# IMPORTANT: Source Code Access

**Local source files are not present.** Your workspace does not contain source code. You **MUST** use Sourcegraph MCP tools to discover, read, and understand code before making any changes.

Use `sg_list_repos` to discover available repositories before searching.


## Required Workflow

1. **Search first** — Use MCP tools to find relevant files and understand existing patterns
2. **Read remotely** — Use `sg_read_file` to read full file contents from Sourcegraph
3. **Edit locally** — Use Edit, Write, and Bash to create or modify files in your working directory
4. **Verify locally** — Run tests with Bash to check your changes

## Tool Selection

| Goal | Tool |
|------|------|
| Exact symbol/string | `sg_keyword_search` |
| Concepts/semantic search | `sg_nls_search` |
| Trace usage/callers | `sg_find_references` |
| See implementation | `sg_go_to_definition` |
| Read full file | `sg_read_file` |
| Browse structure | `sg_list_files` |
| Find repos | `sg_list_repos` |
| Search commits | `sg_commit_search` |
| Track changes | `sg_diff_search` |
| Compare versions | `sg_compare_revisions` |

**Decision logic:**
1. Know the exact symbol? → `sg_keyword_search`
2. Know the concept, not the name? → `sg_nls_search`
3. Need definition of a symbol? → `sg_go_to_definition`
4. Need all callers/references? → `sg_find_references`
5. Need full file content? → `sg_read_file`

## Scoping (Always Do This)

```
repo:^github.com/ORG/REPO$           # Exact repo (preferred)
repo:github.com/ORG/                 # All repos in org
file:.*\.ts$                         # TypeScript only
file:src/api/                        # Specific directory
```

Start narrow. Expand only if results are empty.

## Efficiency Rules

- Chain searches logically: search → read → references → definition
- Don't re-search for the same pattern; use results from prior calls
- Prefer `sg_keyword_search` over `sg_nls_search` when you have exact terms
- Read 2-3 related files before synthesising, rather than one at a time
- Don't read 20+ remote files without writing code — once you understand the pattern, start implementing

## If Stuck

If MCP search returns no results:
1. Broaden the search query (synonyms, partial identifiers)
2. Try `sg_nls_search` for semantic matching
3. Use `sg_list_files` to browse the directory structure
4. Use `sg_list_repos` to verify the repository name

# Envoy xDS v2 to v3 API Migration

## Your Task

Find all C++ source files in envoyproxy/envoy that implement both xDS v2 and v3 API handling: the versioned proto type conversion, the v2-to-v3 field renames (e.g., DiscoveryRequest), and the dual-version subscription handling in the ADS gRPC server.

## Context

You are working on a codebase task involving repos from the migration domain.

The local `/workspace/` directory contains: sg-evals/envoy--v1.31.2, sg-evals/data-plane-api--84e84367, sg-evals/go-control-plane--71637ad6, sg-evals/grpc--957dba5e.

Perfect! I've completed a comprehensive analysis of the Envoy xDS v2 to v3 API migration implementation. Here's a summary of my findings:

## Summary

I've identified all the critical C++ source files in envoyproxy/envoy (v1.31.2) that implement xDS v2 and v3 API handling:

### Key Components Found:

1. **Type URL Mapping** (`source/common/config/type_to_endpoint.cc`)
   - Maps resource type URLs to v3 gRPC service discovery methods
   - Functions: `deltaGrpcMethod()`, `sotwGrpcMethod()`, `restMethod()`

2. **ADS gRPC Mux Implementation** (`source/extensions/config_subscription/grpc/xds_mux/grpc_mux_impl.cc`)
   - `GrpcMuxSotw` and `GrpcMuxDelta` classes for dual-version subscription handling
   - Implements multiplexing of multiple resource subscriptions on single gRPC stream

3. **Subscription State Management**
   - **SotW**: `source/extensions/config_subscription/grpc/xds_mux/sotw_subscription_state.cc` - handles `DiscoveryRequest`/`DiscoveryResponse` (v3)
   - **Delta**: `source/extensions/config_subscription/grpc/xds_mux/delta_subscription_state.cc` - handles `DeltaDiscoveryRequest`/`DeltaDiscoveryResponse` (v3)

4. **Proto Field Renaming & Versioning**
   - v3 proto definitions include `(udpa.annotations.versioning).previous_message_type` pointing to v2 equivalents
   - Examples: `DiscoveryRequest` (from `envoy.api.v2.DiscoveryRequest`), `DeltaDiscoveryRequest`

5. **API Version Validation** (`source/common/config/utility.h`)
   - `checkTransportVersion()` enforces v3-only transport (v2 is deprecated)
   - `ApiVersion` enum defines V2=1 (deprecated), V3=2

The answer file has been created at `/workspace/answer.json` with complete documentation of all relevant files, symbols, and implementation details.

Each package is independently versioned with a protobuf semantic\\n12: versioning scheme based on https://cloud.google.com/apis/design/versioning.\\n13: \\n14: The major version for a package is captured in its name (and directory structure). protocols. Key findings:\\n\\n**Type URL to Service Mapping (source/common/config/type_to_endpoint.cc):** This file implements the critical conversion from resource type URLs (e.g., 'type.googleapis.com/envoy.config.route.v3.RouteConfiguration') to v3 gRPC service methods. The typeUrlToV3ServiceMap() function explicitly enumerates all v3 service discovery services including RouteDiscoveryService, ClusterDiscoveryService, EndpointDiscoveryService, ListenerDiscoveryService, RuntimeDiscoveryService, SecretDiscoveryService, ScopedRoutesDiscoveryService, VirtualHostDiscoveryService, LocalityEndpointDiscoveryService, and ExtensionConfigDiscoveryService. Functions deltaGrpcMethod() and sotwGrpcMethod() map resource types to their respective gRPC endpoints.\\n\\n**ADS gRPC Server and Mux Implementation:** The xds_mux/grpc_mux_impl.cc implements both GrpcMuxSotw and GrpcMuxDelta classes that inherit from GrpcMuxImpl. These are templated classes parameterized by subscription state type and request/response message types (either envoy::service::discovery::v3::DiscoveryRequest/DiscoveryResponse for SotW or envoy::service::discovery::v3::DeltaDiscoveryRequest/DeltaDiscoveryResponse for Delta). The dual-version subscription handling multiplexes multiple resource subscriptions on a single gRPC stream.\\n\\n**Subscription State Management:** The sotw_subscription_state.cc implements SotwSubscriptionState which inherits from BaseSubscriptionState<envoy::service::discovery::v3::DiscoveryResponse, envoy::service::discovery::v3::DiscoveryRequest>. The handleGoodResponse() function processes v3 DiscoveryResponse messages. Similarly, delta_subscription_state.h/.cc in the xds_mux directory implements DeltaSubscriptionState for delta protocol handling with v3 DeltaDiscoveryResponse/DeltaDiscoveryRequest types. The addResourceStateFromServer() function processes v3 Resource messages from delta responses.\\n\\n**v2 to v3 Versioning:** The utility.h file contains checkTransportVersion() which validates and enforces v3-only transport (V2 is deprecated). The api_version.h defines ApiVersion enum with V2 (deprecated, value 1) and V3 (value 2). Proto annotations in api/envoy/service/discovery/v3/discovery.proto show versioning migration with (udpa.annotations.versioning).previous_message_type pointing to v2 equivalents (e.g., 'envoy.api.v2.DiscoveryRequest').\\n\\n**Proto Field Mappings:** The v3 discovery.proto defines DiscoveryRequest with version_info field (from v2), and updated field names in v3 like resource_names_subscribe in DeltaDiscoveryRequest. Both SotW and Delta message types are fully v3 with no inline v2 handling - the v2 to v3 conversion happens at the proto compilation stage and configuration validation layer.\\n\\n**Configuration Subscription Factory:** The grpc_subscription_impl.cc creates GrpcSubscriptionImpl instances that use the GrpcMux (either legacy or unified). The factory pattern in grpc_subscription_factory.cc creates either SotwGrpcMuxFactory or DeltaGrpcMuxFactory based on transport_api_version and api_type configuration, delegating actual mux implementation selection to the unified GrpcMuxSotw or GrpcMuxDelta classes in xds_mux/grpc_mux_impl.cc.\\n\\nThis architecture cleanly separates v3 protocol handling (on the wire) from internal subscription state management, with type_to_endpoint.cc serving as the central mapping point for resource type discovery across all xDS APIs.\"\n}\n",
